      (phi psi : Pattern) 
      (X : svar) {struct phi} : Pattern :=
      match phi with
      | patt_free_evar x => patt_free_evar x

          if decide (X = X')
          then psi
          else patt_free_svar X'
      | patt_bound_evar x => patt_bound_evar x
      | patt_bound_svar X' =>
          patt_bound_svar X'
      | patt_sym sigma => patt_sym sigma
      | phi1 $ phi2 =>
          free_svar_subst phi1 psi X $
          free_svar_subst phi2 psi X

          free_svar_subst phi1 psi X --->
          free_svar_subst phi2 psi X

          ex , free_svar_subst phi' psi X

          mu , free_svar_subst phi' psi X
